        yConversion?: NoiseConversionParams,
    }
    export interface TerrainMaterial {
        // (undocumented)
        setBase(id: number, data: number): TerrainMaterial;
        // (undocumented)
        setCover(id: number, data: number): TerrainMaterial;
        // (undocumented)
        setDiffuse(value: number): TerrainMaterial;
        // (undocumented)
        setFilling(width: number, id: number, data: number): TerrainMaterial;
        // (undocumented)
        setSurface(width: number, id: number, data: number): TerrainMaterial;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface TerrainMaterialParams {
        // (undocumented)
        base?: MaterialBlockData,
        // (undocumented)
        cover?: MaterialBlockData,
        // (undocumented)
        diffuse?: number
        // (undocumented)
        filling?: MaterialBlockData,
        // (undocumented)
        noise?: NoiseOctaveParams | NoiseLayerParams | NoiseGeneratorParams,
        // (undocumented)
        surface?: MaterialBlockData,
    }
    export function transfer(entity: number, dimensionId: number): void;
    // (undocumented)
    export type Vec2Data =
    [number, number] |
        { x: number, y: number } |
    number
    // (undocumented)
    export type Vec3Data =
    [number, number, number] |
        { x: number, y: number, z: number } |
    number;
}

            attack_rate?: number;
            target?: number;
        });
    }

        constructor(customPrototype: EntityAIClass.EntityAIPrototype & {
            speed?: number;
            jumpVel?: number;
            rotateSpeed?: number;
            rotateRatio?: number;
            rotateHead?: boolean;
            denyY?: boolean;
            target?: Vector;
            targetEntity?: number;
        });
    }
    export class Idle extends EntityAIClass {
        constructor(customPrototype: EntityAIClass.EntityAIPrototype);
    }
    export class Panic extends EntityAIClass {
        constructor(customPrototype: EntityAIClass.WanderLikeAIPrototype);
    }
    export class PanicWatcher extends EntityAIClass {
        constructor(customPrototype: EntityAIClass.EntityAIPrototype & {
            panic_time?: number;
            priority_panic?: number;
            priority_default?: number;
            name?: string;
        });
    }
    export class Swim extends EntityAIClass {
        constructor(customPrototype: EntityAIClass.EntityAIPrototype & {
            velocity?: number;
        });
    }
    export class Wander extends EntityAIClass {
        constructor(customPrototype: EntityAIClass.WanderLikeAIPrototype & {
            delay_weight?: number;
        });
    }
}

// @public
export namespace ICRender {
    	const MODE_INCLUDE = 0;
    	const MODE_EXCLUDE = 1;
    	export function AND(...conditions: CONDITION[]): CONDITION;
    	export function BLOCK(x: number, y: number, z: number, group: ICRender.Group, exclude: boolean): CONDITION;
    	export interface CollisionEntry {

        // (undocumented)
        export interface Source {
            // (undocumented)
            apiInstance: any;
            // (undocumented)
            readonly gameVersion: any;
            // (undocumented)
            json: org.json.JSONObject;
            // (undocumented)
            optimizationLevel: number;
            // (undocumented)
            path: string;
            // (undocumented)
            setAPI(api: any): void;
            // (undocumented)
            setOptimizationLevel(level: number): void;
            // (undocumented)
            setPath(path: string): void;
            // (undocumented)
            setSourceName(sourceName: string): void;
            // (undocumented)
            setSourceType(type: SourceType): void;
            // (undocumented)
            sourceName: string;
            // (undocumented)
            sourceType: SourceType;
        }
    }
    export type BuildType = number;
    // (undocumented)
    export interface CompiledSources {
        // (undocumented)
        addCompiledSource(name: string, file: java.io.File, className: string): void;
        // (undocumented)
        getCompiledSourceFilesFor(name: string): java.io.File[];
        // (undocumented)
        getTargetCompilationFile(sourcePath: string): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        reset(): void;
        // (undocumented)
        saveSourceList(): void;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface ModJsAdapter {
        [key: string]: any
        // (undocumented)
        buildConfig: BuildConfig;
        // (undocumented)
        config: Config;
        // (undocumented)
        configureMultiplayer(name: string, version: string, isClientOnly: boolean): void;
        // (undocumented)
        createCompiledSources(): CompiledSources;
        // (undocumented)
        dir: string;
        // (undocumented)
        getBuildType(): BuildType;
        // (undocumented)
        getConfig(): Config;
        // (undocumented)
        getFormattedAPIName(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getGuiIcon(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getInfoProperty(name: string): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getModPack(): ModPack.ModPack;
        // (undocumented)
        getModPackLocationName(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getMultiplayerName(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getMultiplayerVersion(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getName(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getVersion(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        isClientOnly(): boolean;
        // (undocumented)
        isConfiguredForMultiplayer(): boolean;
        // (undocumented)
        isEnabled: boolean;
        // (undocumented)
        isModRunning: boolean;
        // (undocumented)
        onImport(): void;
        // (undocumented)
        runCustomSource(name: string, additionalScope: any): void;
        // (undocumented)
        RunLauncherScripts(): void;
        // (undocumented)
        RunMod(additionalScope: any): void;
        // (undocumented)
        RunPreloaderScripts(): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setBuildType(type: BuildType): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setBuildType(type: "release" | "develop"): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setModPackAndLocation(pack: ModPack.ModPack, locationName: string): void;
    }
    export type ResourceDirType = number;
    export type SourceType = number;
}

    api: object
    ) => void): void;

    export function addTexturePack(path: any): void;

    // Warning: (tsdoc-escape-greater-than) The ">" character should be escaped using a backslash to avoid confusion with an HTML tag
    export function cloneObject<T extends object>(source: T, deep?: boolean, rec?: number): T;
    export function debugCloneObject<T>(source: T, deep?: boolean, rec?: number): T | string;
    // @deprecated (undocumented)
    export function getModByName(modName: string): void;
    // @deprecated (undocumented)
    export function getModList(): void;
    // @deprecated (undocumented)
    export function getModPEList(): void;
    export function inheritPrototypes<K extends object, T extends object>
    (source: K, target: T): K & T;
    // @deprecated (undocumented)
    export function isModLoaded(modName: string): void;
    // @deprecated
    export interface ModDocumentation {
        name: string,
        props: object
    }
    // Warning: (tsdoc-param-tag-with-invalid-name) The @param block should be followed by a valid parameter name: The identifier cannot non-word characters
    // Warning: (tsdoc-param-tag-with-invalid-name) The @param block should be followed by a valid parameter name: The identifier cannot non-word characters
    export function registerAPI(name: string, api: object, descr?: { name?: string, props?: object }): void;

    // @deprecated (undocumented)
    export function requireAPIdoc(name: string): ModDocumentation;

// @public (undocumented)
export namespace ModPack {
    // (undocumented)
    export interface DirectoryExtractStrategy extends IDirectoryAssignable {
        // (undocumented)
        getEntryName(str: string, file: java.io.File): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getFilesToExtract(): java.util.List<java.io.File>;
        // (undocumented)
        getFullEntryName(file: java.io.File): string;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface DirectoryRequestStrategy extends IDirectoryAssignable {
        // (undocumented)
        assure(location: string, name: string): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        get(str: string): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        get(str: string, str2: string): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        getAll(str: string): java.util.List<java.io.File>;
        // (undocumented)
        getAllFiles(): java.util.List<java.io.File>;
        // (undocumented)
        getAllLocations(): java.util.List<string>;
        // (undocumented)
        remove(location: string, name: string): boolean;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface DirectorySetRequestHandler {
        // (undocumented)
        add(dir: ModPackDirectory): void;
        // (undocumented)
        get(location: string, name: string): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        get(location: string): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        getAllAtLocation(location: string): java.util.List<java.io.File>;
        // (undocumented)
        getAllLocations(): java.util.List<string>;
        // (undocumented)
        getDirectories(): java.util.List<ModPackDirectory>;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface DirectoryUpdateStrategy extends IDirectoryAssignable {
        // (undocumented)
        beginUpdate(): void;
        // (undocumented)
        finishUpdate(): void;
        // (undocumented)
        updateFile(str: string, stream: java.io.InputStream): void;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface IDirectoryAssignable {
        // (undocumented)
        assignToDirectory(dir: ModPackDirectory): void;
        // (undocumented)
        getAssignedDirectory(): ModPackDeclaredDirectory;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface ModPack {
        // (undocumented)
        addDirectory(directory: ModPackDirectory): ModPack;
        // (undocumented)
        getAllDirectories(): java.util.List<ModPackDirectory>;
        // (undocumented)
        getDirectoriesOfType(type: ModPackDirectoryType): java.util.List<ModPackDirectory>;
        // (undocumented)
        getDirectoryOfType(type: ModPackDirectoryType): ModPackDirectory;
        // (undocumented)
        getIconFile(): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        getJsAdapter(): ModPackJsAdapter;
        // (undocumented)
        getManifest(): ModPackManifest;
        // (undocumented)
        getManifestFile(): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        getPreferences(): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        getRequestHandler(type: ModPackDirectoryType): DirectorySetRequestHandler;
        // (undocumented)
        getRootDirectory(): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        reloadAndValidateManifest(): boolean;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface ModPackDeclaredDirectory {
        // (undocumented)
        getPath(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getType(): ModPackDeclaredDirectoryType;
        // (undocumented)
        readonly path: string;
        // (undocumented)
        readonly type: ModPackDeclaredDirectoryType;
    }
    export type ModPackDeclaredDirectoryType = number;
    // (undocumented)
    export interface ModPackDirectory {
        // (undocumented)
        assignToModPack(pack: ModPack): void;
        // (undocumented)
        assureDirectoryRoot(): boolean;
        // (undocumented)
        getExtractStrategy(): DirectoryExtractStrategy;
        // (undocumented)
        getLocalPathFromEntry(entryName: string): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getLocation(): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        getPathPattern(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getPathPatternRegex(): java.util.regex.Pattern;
        // (undocumented)
        getRequestStrategy(): DirectoryRequestStrategy;
        // (undocumented)
        getType(): ModPackDirectoryType;
        // (undocumented)
        getUpdateStrategy(): DirectoryUpdateStrategy;
    }
    export type ModPackDirectoryType = number;
    export interface ModPackJsAdapter {
        // (undocumented)
        getAllDirectories(): ModPackDirectory[];
        // (undocumented)
        getDirectoriesOfType(type: string): ModPackDirectory[];
        // (undocumented)
        getDirectoryOfType(type: string): ModPackDirectory;
        // (undocumented)
        getManifest(): ModPackManifest;
        // (undocumented)
        getModPack(): ModPack;
        // (undocumented)
        getModsDirectoryPath(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getPreferences(): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        getRequestHandler(type: string): DirectorySetRequestHandler;
        // (undocumented)
        getRootDirectory(): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        getRootDirectoryPath(): string;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface ModPackManifest {
        // (undocumented)
        createDeclaredDirectoriesForModPack(pack: ModPack): java.util.List<ModPackDirectory>;
        // (undocumented)
        edit(): ModPackManifestEditor;
        // (undocumented)
        getAuthor(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getDeclaredDirectories(): java.util.List<ModPackDeclaredDirectory>;
        // (undocumented)
        getDescription(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getDisplayedName(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getPackName(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        getVersionCode(): number;
        // (undocumented)
        getVersionName(): string;
        // (undocumented)
        loadFile(file: java.io.File): void;
        // (undocumented)
        loadInputStream(stream: java.io.InputStream): void;
        // (undocumented)
        loadJson(json: org.json.JSONObject): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setAuthor(author: string): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setDescription(descr: string): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setDisplayedName(name: string): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setPackName(name: string): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setVersionCode(code: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setVersionName(name: string): void;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface ModPackManifestEditor {
        // (undocumented)
        addIfMissing(key: string, value: any): ModPackManifestEditor;
        // (undocumented)
        commit(): void;
        // (undocumented)
        put(key: string, value: any): ModPackManifestEditor;
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export interface ModPackPreferences {
        // (undocumented)
        getBoolean(key: string, fallback: boolean): boolean;
        // (undocumented)
        getDouble(key: string, fallback: number): number;
        // (undocumented)
        getFile(): java.io.File;
        // (undocumented)
        getInt(key: string, fallback: number): number;
        // (undocumented)
        getLong(key: string, fallback: number): number;
        // (undocumented)
        getModPack(): ModPack;
        // (undocumented)
        getString(key: string, fallback: string): string;
        // (undocumented)
        reload(): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        save(): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        setBoolean(key: string, value: boolean): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        setDouble(key: string, value: number): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        setInt(key: string, value: number): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        setLong(key: string, value: number): ModPackPreferences;
        // (undocumented)
        setString(key: string, value: string): ModPackPreferences;
    }
}

    export function getClientForPlayer(player: number): NetworkClient;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getConnectedClients(): native.Array<NetworkClient>;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getConnectedPlayers(): native.Array<number>;
    // (undocumented)
    export function inRemoteWorld(): boolean;
    export function localToServerId(id: string | number): number;
    export function sendServerMessage(message: string): void;
    export function sendToAllClients(name: string, packetData: object): void;
    export function sendToServer(name: string, packetData: object): void;
    export function serverToLocalId(id: string | number): number;
}

// @public
export namespace Particles {
    export function addFarParticle(type: number, x: number, y: number, z: number, vx: number, vy: number, vz: number, data?: number): void;
    export function addParticle(type: number, x: number, y: number, z: number, vx: number, vy: number, vz: number, data?: number): void;
    export interface AnimatorDescription extends IAnimatorDescription {
        end?: number;
        start?: number;
    }
    export interface ColorAnimatorDescription extends IAnimatorDescription {
        end?: [number, number, number, number];
        start?: [number, number, number, number];
    }
    // (undocumented)
    export function getParticleTypeById(id: number): ParticleType;
    export interface IAnimatorDescription {
        fadeIn?: number;
        fadeOut?: number;
        period?: number;
    }
    export class ParticleAnimator {
        constructor(period: number, fadeInTime: number, fadeInValue: number, fadeOutTime: number, fadeOutValue: number);
        constructor(descriptor: AnimatorDescription);
    }
    export interface ParticleDescription {
        acceleration?: [number, number, number];
        addLifetimeAfterImpact?: number;
        animators?: {
            size?: AnimatorDescription;
            alpha?: AnimatorDescription;
            texture?: AnimatorDescription;
            icon?: AnimatorDescription;
            color?: ColorAnimatorDescription;
        }
        collision?: boolean;
        color?: [number, number, number, number];
        // (undocumented)
        color2?: [number, number, number, number];
        emitters?: {
            idle?: SubEmitterDescription;
            impact?: SubEmitterDescription;
            death?: SubEmitterDescription;
        }
        framesX?: number;
        framesY?: number;
        friction?: {
            air?: number;
            block?: number;
        }
        isUsingBlockLight?: boolean;
        keepVelocityAfterImpact?: boolean;
        lifetime: [number, number];
        rebuildDelay?: number;
        render?: number;
        size: [number, number];
        texture: string;
        velocity?: [number, number, number];
    }
    export class ParticleEmitter {
        constructor(x: number, y: number, z: number);
        attachTo(entity: number): void;
        attachTo(entity: number, x: number, y: number, z: number): void;
        detach(): void;
        emit(type: number, data: number, x: number, y: number, z: number): void;
        emit(type: number, data: number, x: number, y: number, z: number, vx: number, vy: number, vz: number): void;
        emit(type: number, data: number, x: number, y: number, z: number, vx: number, vy: number, vz: number, ax: number, ay: number, az: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        getPosition(): Vector;
        // (undocumented)
        getPositionArray(): [number, number, number];
        move(x: number, y: number, z: number): void;
        moveTo(x: number, y: number, z: number): void;
        release(): void;
        setEmitRelatively(enable: boolean): void
        setVelocity(x: number, y: number, z: number): void;
        stop(): void;
    }
    export class ParticleSubEmitter {
        constructor(chance: number, count: number, type: number, data: number);
        constructor(descriptor: SubEmitterDescription);
        // (undocumented)
        setKeepEmitter(keepEmitter: boolean): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setKeepVelocity(keepVelocity: boolean): void;
        setRandomVelocity(maxRandomVelocity: number): void;
    }
    export class ParticleType {
        constructor(textureName: string, minU: number, minV: number, maxU: number, maxV: number, textureCountHorizontal: number, textureCountVertical: number, isUsingBlockLight: boolean);
        constructor(locationName: string, isUsingBlockLight: boolean, uv: number[], textureCountHorizontal: number, textureCountVertical: number);
        constructor(descriptor: ParticleDescription);
        // (undocumented)
        getId(): number;
        // (undocumented)
        setAnimator(name: "size" | "icon" | "alpha" | "color", animator: ParticleAnimator): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setCollisionParams(collision: boolean, keepVelocityAfterImpact: boolean, addLifetimeAfterImpact: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setColor(r: number, g: number, b: number, a: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setColor(r: number, g: number, b: number, a: number, r2: number, g2: number, b2: number, a2: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setDefaultAcceleration(x: number, y: number, z: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setDefaultVelocity(x: number, y: number, z: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setFriction(air: number, block: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setLifetime(min: number, max: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setRebuildDelay(delay: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setRenderType(renderType: 0 | 1 | 2): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setSize(min: number, max: number): void;
        // (undocumented)
        setSubEmitter(name: "idle" | "impact" | "death", emitter: ParticleSubEmitter): void;
    }
    export function registerParticleType(descriptor: ParticleDescription): number;
    export interface SubEmitterDescription {
        chance?: number;
        count?: number;
        data?: number;
        keepEmitter?: boolean;
        keepVelocity?: boolean;
        randomize?: number;
        type: number;
    }
}

    export function getBlockData(blockID: number): BlockData | undefined;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getBlockDestroyLevel(blockID: number): number;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getBlockMaterial(blockID: number): Nullable<BlockMaterial>;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getBlockMaterialName(blockID: number): Nullable<string>;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getCarriedToolData(): any;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getCarriedToolLevel(): number;
    export function getDestroyTimeViaTool(fullBlock: Tile, toolItem: ItemInstance, coords: Callback.ItemUseCoordinates, ignoreNative?: boolean): number;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getEnchantExtraData(extra?: ItemExtraData): EnchantData;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getToolData(itemID: number): Nullable<ToolParams>;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getToolLevel(itemID: number): number;
    // (undocumented)
    export function getToolLevelViaBlock(itemID: number, blockID: number): number;
    // @deprecated (undocumented)
    export function refresh(): void;
    export function registerBlockDiggingLevel(uid: number, level: number): void;
    export function registerBlockMaterial(uid: number, materialName: string, level?: number, isNative?: boolean): void;
    export function registerBlockMaterialAsArray(materialName: string, UIDs: number[], isNative: boolean): void;
    export function registerSword(id: number, toolMaterial: string | ToolMaterial, params?: ToolParams): void;
    export function registerTool(id: number, toolMaterial: string | ToolMaterial, blockMaterials: string[], params?: ToolParams): void;
    // @internal
    export function resetEngine(): void;
    export interface ToolMaterial {
        damage?: number,
        durability?: number,
        efficiency?: number,
        level?: number
    }
    export interface ToolParams {
        [key: string]: any
        blockMaterials?: { [key: string]: boolean }
        brokenId?: number,
        calcDestroyTime?: (
        tool: ItemInstance,
        coords: Callback.ItemUseCoordinates,
        block: Tile,
        timeData: {
            base: number,
            devider: number,
            modifier: number
        },
        defaultTime: number,
        enchantData?: EnchantData
        ) => number,
        damage?: number,
        // @internal
        isNative?: boolean,
        isWeapon?: boolean,
        modifyEnchant?: (
        enchantData: EnchantData,
        item: ItemInstance,
        coords?: Callback.ItemUseCoordinates,
        block?: Tile
        ) => void,
        onAttack?: (
        item: ItemInstance,
        victim: number,
        attacker: number
        ) => boolean,
        onBroke?: (
        item: ItemInstance
        ) => boolean,
        onDestroy?: (
        item: ItemInstance,
        coords: Callback.ItemUseCoordinates,
        block: Tile,
        player: number
        ) => boolean,
        onMineBlock?: (
        coords: Callback.ItemUseCoordinates,
        carried: ItemInstance,
        fullTile: Tile,
        blockSource: BlockSource,
        player: number
        ) => void,
        toolMaterial?: ToolMaterial,
    }
}
